SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                        trigger sp_activities_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            on sp_activities                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                        declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            l_tags varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                        begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            -- validations                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            if :new.end_date < :new.start_date then                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                raise_application_error(-20111,'End date must be greater than start date');                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            -- adjust tags                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                    for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                        l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                        if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                           exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                        end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                    end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                    if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                       l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                    end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                                :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            -- touch parent                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                            update sp_projects set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.project_id;                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITIES_BIU                        end sp_activities_biu;                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                     trigger sp_activity_types_bd                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                         before delete                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                         on sp_activity_types                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                         for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                     begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                         insert into sp_app_log                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                             (activity, details)                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                         values                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                             ('Deleted Activity Type', :old.activity_type);                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BD                     end sp_activity_types_bd;

SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        on sp_activity_types

SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        if :new.is_active_yn is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                           :new.is_active_yn := 'Y';                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            insert into sp_app_log                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                (activity, details)                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                ('Added Activity Type' , :new.activity_type);                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        elsif updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.activity_type,:new.activity_type) then                                                                                                                                                         
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                insert into sp_app_log                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    (activity, details)                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    ('Updated Activity Type' , 'Changed "'||:old.activity_type ||'" to "'||:new.activity_type||'"');                                                                                                                             
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.STATIC_ID,:new.STATIC_ID) then                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                insert into sp_app_log                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    (activity, details)                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    ('Updated Activity Type' , :new.activity_type||': changed STATIC_ID from "'||:old.STATIC_ID||'" to "'||:new.STATIC_ID||'"');                                                                                                 
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.IS_PROJECT_YN,:new.IS_PROJECT_YN) then                                                                                                                                                         
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                insert into sp_app_log                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    (activity, details)                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    ('Updated Activity Type' , :new.activity_type||': changed IS_PROJECT from "'||:old.IS_PROJECT_YN||'" to "'||:new.IS_PROJECT_YN||'"');                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.IS_DEFAULT_YN,:new.IS_DEFAULT_YN) then                                                                                                                                                         
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                insert into sp_app_log                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    (activity, details)                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    ('Updated Activity Type' , :new.activity_type||': changed IS_DEFAULT from "'||:old.IS_DEFAULT_YN||'" to "'||:new.IS_DEFAULT_YN||'"');                                                                                        
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.IS_ACTIVE_YN,:new.IS_ACTIVE_YN) then                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                insert into sp_app_log                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    (activity, details)                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                                    ('Updated Activity Type' , :new.activity_type||': changed IS_ACTIVE from "'||:old.IS_ACTIVE_YN||'" to "'||:new.IS_ACTIVE_YN||'"');                                                                                           
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                        end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_ACTIVITY_TYPES_BIU                    end sp_activity_types_biu;

SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                         TRIGGER  sp_countries_biu

SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                                :new.created := localtimestamp;                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                                :new.created_by := nvl(wwv_flow.g_user,user);                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                                :new.updated := localtimestamp;                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                                :new.updated_by := nvl(wwv_flow.g_user,user);                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            if inserting or updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                                :new.updated := localtimestamp;                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                                :new.updated_by := nvl(wwv_flow.g_user,user);                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            if :new.display_yn is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                               :new.display_yn := 'Y';                                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            if :new.quick_pick_yn is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                               :new.quick_pick_yn := 'N';                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_COUNTRIES_BIU                         end sp_countries_biu;

SP_INITIATIVES_AI                        trigger sp_initiatives_ai                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                            after insert                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                            on sp_initiatives                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                            for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                        declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                            l_new_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                        begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                            for c1 in (select AREA r from SP_AREAS x where x.id = :new.AREA_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                            insert into sp_initiative_history                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                                (initiative_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                            values                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                                (:new.id, 'INITIATIVE', 'CREATE', l_new_value||': '||:new.initiative, sysdate, lower(:new.created_by));                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_AI                        end sp_initiatives_ai;                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                        trigger sp_initiatives_bd                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            before delete                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            on sp_initiatives                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                        declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            l_old_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                        begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            update sp_areas set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :old.updated_by where id = :old.area_id;                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            for c1 in (select AREA r from SP_AREAS x where x.id = :old.AREA_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            insert into sp_initiative_history                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                                (initiative_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                            values                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                                (:old.id, 'INITIATIVE', 'DELETE', l_old_value||': '||:old.initiative, sysdate, lower(coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user)));                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BD                        end sp_initiatives_bd;                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                       trigger sp_initiatives_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           on sp_initiatives                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                       declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           l_tags        varchar2(4000);                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           l_old_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           l_new_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           l_changed_by  varchar2(255)  := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                       begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           if :new.SPONSOR_ID is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                              for c1 in (select OWNER_ID from SP_AREAS f where f.id = :new.AREA_ID and owner_id is not null) loop                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                  :new.SPONSOR_ID := c1.owner_id;                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                              end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           -- short ID used as an alternative to long numeric ID primary key column                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           if :new.friendly_identifier is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                              :new.friendly_identifier := sp_util.compress_int(sp_seq.nextval);                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           -- used to provide friendly URLs                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.initiative,:new.initiative) then                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                              :new.initiative_url_name := ltrim(rtrim(replace(replace(REGEXP_REPLACE(translate(substr(:new.initiative,1,80),'()+%$&^!@[];:"?/~!-+_.<>','                        '),'\s+', ' '), '''', ''),' ','-'),'-'),'-');                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           -- status scale                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           if :new.status_scale is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                              :new.status_scale := 'A';                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                          exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                      l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          if :new.hidden_by_default_yn is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                             :new.hidden_by_default_yn := 'N';                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                          update sp_areas set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.area_id;                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                           if updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               l_changed_by := lower(:new.updated_by);                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.initiative,:new.initiative) then                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   insert into sp_initiative_history                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       (initiative_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value,changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       (:new.id, 'INITIATIVE', 'UPDATE', :old.initiative, :new.initiative, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.area_id,:new.area_id) then                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   for c1 in (select AREA r from SP_AREAS x where x.id = :old.AREA_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   for c1 in (select AREA r from SP_AREAS x where x.id = :new.AREA_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   insert into sp_initiative_history                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       (initiative_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value,changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       (:new.id, 'AREA', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                                
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.objective,:new.objective) then                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   insert into sp_initiative_history                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       (initiative_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value,changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                       (:new.id, 'OBJECTIVE', 'UPDATE', :old.objective, :new.objective, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                               if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.sponsor_id,:new.sponsor_id) then                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVES_BIU                                   for c1 in (select lower(email) r from SP_TEAM_MEMBERS x where x.id = :old.sponsor_id) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;

SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD          trigger sp_initiative_approval_chain_bd                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              before delete

SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD          declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              l_initiative_id  number;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              l_approval_type  varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              l_old_value      varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD          begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              --

SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              update sp_initiative_approvals set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :old.updated_by where id = :old.initiative_approval_id;                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              for c1 in (select x.initiative_id, t.approval_type                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD                           from sp_initiative_approvals x, sp_approval_types t                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD                          where x.id = :old.initiative_approval_id                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD                            and x.approval_type_id = t.id                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD                        ) loop l_initiative_id := c1.initiative_id; l_approval_type := c1.approval_type; end loop;                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              for c1 in (select lower(email) r from SP_TEAM_MEMBERS x where x.id = :old.team_member_id) loop l_old_value := :old.approval_seq||'-'||c1.r; end loop;                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD              insert into sp_initiative_history

SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD                  (l_initiative_id, 'INITIATIVE_APPROVAL', 'DELETE',                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD                   l_approval_type||' - '||l_old_value||' ('||decode(:old.active_yn,'Y','Active','Inactive')||')',                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD                   sysdate, lower(coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user)));                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVE_APPROVAL_CHAIN_BD          end sp_initiative_approval_chain_bd;
