SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU              trigger sp_initiative_documents_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  on sp_initiative_documents                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU              declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  l_tags varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU              begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  :new.tags := upper(:new.tags);                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  update sp_initiatives set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.initiative_id;                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                  if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                          for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                              l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                              if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                 exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                              end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                          end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                          if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                      :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INITIATIVE_DOCUMENTS_BIU              end sp_initiative_documents_biu;

SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_COMMENTS_BD           trigger sp_init_focus_area_comments_bd                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_COMMENTS_BD               before delete

SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_COMMENTS_BD               for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_COMMENTS_BD           begin

SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU         trigger sp_init_focus_area_documents_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             on sp_init_focus_area_documents                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU         declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             l_tags varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU         begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             :new.tags := upper(:new.tags);                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             update sp_initiative_focus_areas set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.init_focus_area_id;                                                                                                                 
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 insert into sp_init_focus_area_history                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     (init_focus_area_id, attribute_column, change_type, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                           
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     (:new.init_focus_area_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'CREATE', :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.created_by));                                                                                                                        
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             elsif updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 insert into sp_init_focus_area_history                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     (init_focus_area_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     (:new.init_focus_area_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'UPDATE', :old.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.updated_by));                                                                                                
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_INIT_FOCUS_AREA_DOCUMENTS_BIU         end sp_init_focus_area_documents_biu;
