SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              on sp_projects                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                          declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              l_old_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              l_new_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              l_changed_by  varchar2(255)  := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                   
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              l_old_clob    clob;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              l_new_clob    clob;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              l_tags        varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                          begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- maintain tracking columns                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  :new.created_by := l_changed_by;                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if sp_globals.g_audit_this then                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  :new.updated_by := l_changed_by;                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- upper project name                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              :new.upper_project_name := upper(:new.project);                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- set external_ticket_identifier and EXTERNAL_TICKET_SYSTEM and external_system_link                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              :new.external_ticket_system     := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              :new.external_ticket_identifier := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              :new.external_system_link       := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              for c1 in (                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  select EXTERNAL_SYSTEM_NAME,                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                         LINK_PATTERN,                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                         TICKET_ID_REGEX,                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                         REQUIRED_INITIATIVE_ID,                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                         replace(replace(replace(replace(regexp_substr(:new.project,ticket_id_regex),':','-'),' ','-'),'<','-'),'>','-') ext_id                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    from SP_EXTERNAL_TICKETING_SYSTEMS                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                   where nvl(IS_ACTIVE_YN,'N') = 'Y'                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     and regexp_substr(:new.project,ticket_id_regex) is not null                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     and (required_initiative_id is null or required_initiative_id = :new.initiative_id)                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                   order by evaulation_sequence                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              ) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     :new.EXTERNAL_TICKET_SYSTEM := c1.EXTERNAL_SYSTEM_NAME;                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     if instr(c1.LINK_PATTERN,'#TICKET_NUMERIC#') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        :new.external_ticket_identifier := c1.ext_id;                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        :new.external_system_link       := replace(c1.LINK_PATTERN,'#TICKET_NUMERIC#',regexp_replace(c1.ext_id,'[^0-9]',''));                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     elsif instr(c1.LINK_PATTERN,'#TICKET#') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        :new.external_ticket_identifier := c1.ext_id;                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        :new.external_system_link       := replace(c1.LINK_PATTERN,'#TICKET#',:new.external_ticket_identifier);                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     else                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        :new.external_ticket_identifier := null;                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        :new.external_system_link       := c1.LINK_PATTERN;                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                     exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                      for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                          l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                          if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                             exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                      end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                      if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                         l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                      end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                  :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- defaults                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if :new.STATUS_SCALE is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 :new.STATUS_SCALE := 'A';                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if :new.ARCHIVED_YN is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 :new.ARCHIVED_YN := 'N';                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- short project ID used as an alturnative to long numeric ID primary key column                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if :new.friendly_identifier is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 :new.friendly_identifier := sp_util.compress_int(sp_seq.nextval);                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- used to provide friendly URLs                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.project,:new.project) then                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 :new.project_url_name := ltrim(rtrim(replace(replace(REGEXP_REPLACE(translate(substr(:new.project,1,80),'()+%$&^!@[];:"?/~!-+_.<>','                        '),'\s+', ' '), '''', ''),' ','-'),'-'),'-');                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              -- change history tracking                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                              if updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 l_changed_by := lower(l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- INITIATIVE_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.INITIATIVE_ID,:new.INITIATIVE_ID) then                                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select INITIATIVE r from SP_INITIATIVES x where x.id = :old.INITIATIVE_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select INITIATIVE r from SP_INITIATIVES x where x.id = :new.INITIATIVE_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'INITIATIVE', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- PROJECT                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.PROJECT,:new.PROJECT) then                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'PROJECT', 'UPDATE', :old.PROJECT, :new.PROJECT, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- DESCRIPTION                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.DESCRIPTION,:new.DESCRIPTION) then                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    l_old_clob := :old.DESCRIPTION;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    l_new_clob := :new.DESCRIPTION;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, old_value_clob, new_value_clob, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'DESCRIPTION', 'UPDATE', dbms_lob.substr(:old.DESCRIPTION,500,1), dbms_lob.substr(:new.DESCRIPTION,500,1), l_old_clob, l_new_clob, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                           
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- OWNER_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.OWNER_ID,:new.OWNER_ID) then                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select lower(email) r from SP_TEAM_MEMBERS x where x.id = :old.owner_id) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select lower(email) r from SP_TEAM_MEMBERS x where x.id = :new.owner_id) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'OWNER', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- TARGET_COMPLETE                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.TARGET_COMPLETE,:new.TARGET_COMPLETE) then                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'TARGET_COMPLETE', 'UPDATE', to_char(:old.TARGET_COMPLETE,'DD-MON-YYYY'), to_char(:new.TARGET_COMPLETE,'DD-MON-YYYY'), sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- STATUS_SCALE                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.status_scale,:new.status_scale) then                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select scale_name from sp_project_scales where :old.status_scale = scale_letter) loop l_old_value := c1.scale_name; end loop;                                                                                           
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select scale_name from sp_project_scales where :new.status_scale = scale_letter) loop l_new_value := c1.scale_name; end loop;                                                                                           
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'STATUS_SCALE', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- PCT_COMPLETE                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.pct_complete,:new.pct_complete) then                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'PCT_COMPLETE', 'UPDATE', :old.pct_complete, :new.pct_complete, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- STATUS                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.status_id,:new.status_id) then                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select status from sp_project_statuses where :old.status_id = id) loop l_old_value := c1.status; end loop;                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select status from sp_project_statuses where :new.status_id = id) loop l_new_value := c1.status; end loop;                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'STATUS', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                                
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- REQUIRES_REVIEWS_YN                                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.requires_reviews_yn,:new.requires_reviews_yn) then                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'REQUIRES_REVIEWS', 'UPDATE', :old.requires_reviews_yn, :new.requires_reviews_yn, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- DUPLICATE_OF_PROJECT_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.duplicate_of_project_id,:new.duplicate_of_project_id) then                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'DUPLICATE_OF_PROJECT_ID', 'UPDATE', :old.duplicate_of_project_id, :new.duplicate_of_project_id, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- PRIORITY_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.priority_id,:new.priority_id) then                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select 'P'||PRIORITY r from SP_PROJECT_PRIORITIES x where x.id = :old.PRIORITY_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select 'P'||PRIORITY r from SP_PROJECT_PRIORITIES x where x.id = :new.PRIORITY_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'PRIORITY', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- RELEASE_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.RELEASE_ID,:new.RELEASE_ID) then                                                                                                                                                                
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select RELEASE_TRAIN||' '||RELEASE r from SP_RELEASE_TRAINS x where x.id = :old.RELEASE_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select RELEASE_TRAIN||' '||RELEASE r from SP_RELEASE_TRAINS x where x.id = :new.RELEASE_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                         
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'RELEASE', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- TAGS                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.tags,:new.tags) then                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (:new.id, 'TAGS', 'UPDATE', :old.tags, :new.tags, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 -- PROJECT_GROUP                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.PROJECT_GROUP_ID,:new.PROJECT_GROUP_ID) then                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select GROUP_NAME r from SP_PROJECT_GROUPS x where x.id = :old.PROJECT_GROUP_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    for c1 in (select GROUP_NAME r from SP_PROJECT_GROUPS x where x.id = :new.PROJECT_GROUP_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                        (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECTS_BIU                                    values

SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        for c1 in (select first_name||' '||last_name||' - '||email x from SP_TEAM_MEMBERS t where t.id = :NEW.TEAM_MEMBER_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.x; end loop;                                                                          
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        for c1 in (select resource_type x from SP_RESOURCE_TYPES t where t.id = :OLD.RESPONSIBILITY_ID) loop l_old_value := l_old_value||' - '||c1.x; end loop;                                                                            
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        for c1 in (select resource_type x from SP_RESOURCE_TYPES t where t.id = :NEW.RESPONSIBILITY_ID) loop l_new_value := l_new_value||' - '||c1.x; end loop;                                                                            
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        -- only log updates that change values                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        if nvl(l_old_value,'x') != nvl(l_new_value,'x') then                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                            insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                                (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                            values                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                                (:new.project_id, 'CONTRIBUTOR', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, lower(:new.updated_by));                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                        end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                  end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECT_CONTRIBUTORS_BIU              end sp_project_contributors_biu;

SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                      for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                  begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                      --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                      -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                      --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                      update sp_projects set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :old.updated_by where id = :old.project_id;                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                      --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                      insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                          (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, changed_on, changed_by)
