SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BD                  end sp_project_documents_bd;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 trigger sp_project_documents_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     on sp_project_documents                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     l_tags varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     :new.tags := upper(:new.tags);                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     update sp_projects set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.project_id;                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                 l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                 if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                    exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                    end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                                   
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (:new.project_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'CREATE', :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.created_by));                                                                                                                                
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     elsif updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         insert into sp_project_history                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (project_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (:new.project_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'UPDATE', :old.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.updated_by));                                                                                                        
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 end sp_project_documents_biu;

SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 trigger sp_release_documents_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     on sp_release_documents                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     l_tags varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                 begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     :new.tags := upper(:new.tags);                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     update sp_release_trains set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.release_id;                                                                                                                                 
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                 l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                 if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                    exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                    end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         insert into sp_release_history                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (release_id, attribute_column, change_type, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                                   
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (:new.release_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'CREATE', :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.created_by));                                                                                                                                
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     elsif updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         insert into sp_release_history                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (release_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                        
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                         values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                             (:new.release_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'UPDATE', :old.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.updated_by));                                                                                                        
SP_RELEASE_DOCUMENTS_BIU                     end if;

SP_TASKS_AI                              trigger sp_tasks_ai                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_AI                                  after insert                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_AI                                  on sp_tasks                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_AI                                  for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_AI                              declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_AI                                  l_type  varchar2(5000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_AI                              begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASKS_AI                                  for c1 in (                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_AI                                      select TASK_TYPE || case when :new.TASK_SUB_TYPE_ID is not null                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_AI                                                               then ': '||(select task_type from sp_task_types                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_AI                                                                            where id = :new.task_sub_type_id)                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_AI                                                               end ||                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_AI                                                          case when :new.task is not null                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASKS_AI                                                               then ' - '||:new.task                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_AI                                                               end  r                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_AI                                        from SP_TASK_TYPES x                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_AI                                       where x.id = :new.TASK_TYPE_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_AI                                  ) loop l_type := substr(c1.r,1,4000); end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_AI                                  insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_AI                                      (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_AI                                  values                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASKS_AI                                      (:new.id, 'TASK', 'CREATE', l_type, sysdate, lower(:new.created_by));                                                                                                                                                                
SP_TASKS_AI                              end sp_tasks_ai;                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BD                              trigger sp_tasks_bd                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BD                                  before delete                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASKS_BD                                  on sp_tasks                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_BD                                  for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BD                              declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BD                                  l_type  varchar2(5000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BD                              begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASKS_BD                                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BD                                  -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BD                                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BD                                  update sp_projects set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :old.updated_by where id = :old.project_id;                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BD                                  --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BD                                  for c1 in (                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_BD                                      select TASK_TYPE || case when :old.TASK_SUB_TYPE_ID is not null                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BD                                                               then ': '||(select task_type from sp_task_types                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BD                                                                            where id = :old.task_sub_type_id)                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_BD                                                               end ||                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BD                                                          case when :old.task is not null                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASKS_BD                                                               then ' - '||:new.task                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BD                                                               end r                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BD                                        from SP_TASK_TYPES x                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BD                                       where x.id = :old.TASK_TYPE_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BD                                  ) loop l_type := substr(c1.r,1,4000); end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BD                                  insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_BD                                      (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BD                                  values                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASKS_BD                                      (:old.id, 'TASK', 'DELETE', l_type, sysdate, lower(coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user)));                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BD                              end sp_tasks_bd;                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                             trigger sp_tasks_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 on sp_tasks                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                             declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 l_old_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 l_new_value   varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 l_changed_by  varchar2(255)  := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 l_tags        varchar2(4000) := null;                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                             begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 -- maintain tracking columns                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_TASKS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 -- maintain status_last_changed                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.status_id,:new.status_id) then                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    :new.status_last_changed_on := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASKS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                         for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_BIU                                             l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                             if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                                exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_TASKS_BIU                                             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BIU                                         end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BIU                                         if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                            l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BIU                                         end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASKS_BIU                                     :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_TASKS_BIU                                end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASKS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 update sp_projects set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.project_id;                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 -- change history tracking                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASKS_BIU                                 if updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    l_changed_by := lower(:new.updated_by);                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    -- PROJECT_ID                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.PROJECT_ID,:new.PROJECT_ID) then                                                                                                                                                                
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       for c1 in (select PROJECT r from SP_PROJECTS x where x.id = :old.PROJECT_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                                   
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       for c1 in (select PROJECT r from SP_PROJECTS x where x.id = :new.PROJECT_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                                   
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASKS_BIU                                           (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                         
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                                           (:new.id, 'PROJECT', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    -- TASK_TYPE                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.TASK_TYPE_ID,:new.TASK_TYPE_ID) then                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       for c1 in (select TASK_TYPE r from SP_TASK_TYPES x where x.id = :old.TASK_TYPE_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       for c1 in (select TASK_TYPE r from SP_TASK_TYPES x where x.id = :new.TASK_TYPE_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASKS_BIU                                           (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                         
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       values                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                                           (:new.id, 'TASK_TYPE', 'UPDATE', l_old_value, l_new_value, sysdate, l_changed_by);                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    -- TASK_SUB_TYPE                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --

SP_TASKS_BIU                                       for c1 in (select TASK_TYPE r from SP_TASK_TYPES x where x.id = :old.TASK_SUB_TYPE_ID) loop l_old_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                         
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       for c1 in (select TASK_TYPE r from SP_TASK_TYPES x where x.id = :new.TASK_SUB_TYPE_ID) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                         
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       insert into sp_task_history

SP_TASKS_BIU                                    end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    -- TASK                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --

SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --

SP_TASKS_BIU                                       for c1 in (select lower(email) r from SP_TEAM_MEMBERS x where x.id = :new.owner_id) loop l_new_value := c1.r; end loop;                                                                                                            
SP_TASKS_BIU                                       insert into sp_task_history

SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --

SP_TASKS_BIU                                    --

SP_TASKS_BIU                                       insert into sp_task_history

SP_TASKS_BIU                                    end if;
