SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                      trigger sp_task_comments_bd                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                          before delete                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                          on sp_task_comments                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                          for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                      begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                          if :old.private_yn = 'N' then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                              -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                              update sp_tasks set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :old.updated_by where id = :old.task_id;                                                                                                                                         
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                              --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                              insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                                  (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, old_value_clob, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                              values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                                  (:old.task_id, 'COMMENT', 'DELETE', dbms_lob.substr(:old.body_no_images,500,1), :old.body_no_images, sysdate, lower(coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user)));                                                     
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BD                      end sp_task_comments_bd;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                     trigger sp_task_comments_biu                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         before insert or update                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         on sp_task_comments                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                     begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                             :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                             :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         if :new.private_yn is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                             :new.private_yn := 'N';                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         update sp_tasks set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.task_id;                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         if inserting and :new.private_yn = 'N' then                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                             insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                                 (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, new_value, new_value_clob, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                             values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                                 (:new.task_id, 'COMMENT', 'CREATE', dbms_lob.substr(:new.body_no_images,500,1), :new.body_no_images, sysdate, lower(:new.created_by));                                                                                           
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         elsif updating and :old.private_yn = 'N' and :new.private_yn = 'N' then                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                             if not sp_value_compare.is_equal(:old.body_no_images,:new.body_no_images) then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                                 insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                                     (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, old_value_clob, new_value_clob, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                                 values                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                                     (:new.task_id, 'COMMENT', 'UPDATE', dbms_lob.substr(:old.body_no_images,500,1), dbms_lob.substr(:new.body_no_images,1), :old.body_no_images, :new.body_no_images, sysdate, lower(:new.updated_by));                          
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                         end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_COMMENTS_BIU                     end sp_task_comments_biu;

SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        -- touch parent table                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        update sp_tasks set updated = sysdate, updated_by = :new.updated_by where id = :new.task_id;                                                                                                                                             
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        -- adjust tag data                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        if :new.tags is not null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            l_tags := trim(upper(:new.tags));                                                                                                                                                                                                    
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            -- remove multiple spaces                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            if instr(l_tags,'  ') > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                for j in 1..10 loop                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                    l_tags := replace(l_tags,'  ',' ');                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                    if instr(l_tags,'  ') = 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                       exit;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                    end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            for i in 1..length(l_tags) loop                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                if i > 2 and substr(l_tags,i,1) = ' ' and substr(l_tags,i-1,1) != ',' then                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                   l_tags := substr(l_tags,1,i-1)||'-'||substr(l_tags,i+1);                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            end loop;                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            :new.tags := l_tags;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                       end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        -- history                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                (:new.task_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'CREATE', :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.created_by));                                                                                                                                   
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        elsif updating then                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            insert into sp_task_history                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                (task_id, attribute_column, change_type, old_value, new_value, changed_on, changed_by)                                                                                                                                           
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                            values                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                                (:new.task_id, 'DOCUMENT', 'UPDATE', :old.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, :new.DOCUMENT_FILENAME, sysdate, lower(:new.updated_by));                                                                                                           
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                        end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TASK_DOCUMENTS_BIU                    end sp_task_documents_biu;

SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          on sp_team_members                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          for each row                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                      declare                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          b integer := 0; -- first dot occurrance                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          e integer := 0; -- first at sign occurrance                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          l integer := 0; -- length between dot and at sign                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                      begin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          if inserting then                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                              :new.created := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                              :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);

SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          :new.updated := sysdate;                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user);                                                                                                                                                                
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          :new.email := lower(:new.email);                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          :new.screen_name := lower(:new.screen_name);                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          if :new.is_current_yn is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                             :new.is_current_yn := 'Y';                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          b := instr(:new.email,'.');                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          e := instr(:new.email,'@');                                                                                                                                                                                                              
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          :new.email_domain := substr(:new.email,e+1);                                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          --                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          if e > 2 and b > 1 and :new.first_name is null and :new.last_name is null then                                                                                                                                                           
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                             l := (e - b) - 1;                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                             if b < e and l > 0 then                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                                 :new.first_name := initcap(substr(:new.email,1,b-1));                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                                 :new.last_name  := initcap(substr(:new.email,b+1,l));                                                                                                                                                                             
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                             end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          if :new.initials is null and :new.first_name is not null and :new.last_name is not null then                                                                                                                                             
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                              :new.initials := nvl(substr(:new.first_name,1,1)||substr(:new.last_name,1,1),'X');                                                                                                                                                   
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          if :new.initials is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                            
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                             :new.initials := 'AA';                                                                                                                                                                                                                
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          if :new.first_name is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                             :new.first_name := 'unknown';                                                                                                                                                                                                         
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          if :new.last_name is null then                                                                                                                                                                                                           
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                             :new.last_name := 'unknown';                                                                                                                                                                                                          
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          end if;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
SP_TEAM_MEMBERS_BIU                          --
